<script>
  $(document).ready(function () {
    $('#viewer_info_button').click(function (e) {
      e.preventDefault();
      var email = $('#viewer_email').val();
      $.ajax
        ({
          type: "POST",
          url: "https://meritnotes.com//healper/new_letter_insert.php",
          data: { "email": email},
          success: function (data) {
            $('.viewer_result').html(data);
            $('#viewerform')[0].reset();
          }
        });
    });
  });
</script>	

<script>
  $(document).ready(function () {
    $('#gdcomment').click(function (e) {
      e.preventDefault();
      var viewerscomments = $('#viewerscomments').val();
      var comment_id = $('#comment_id').val();
      var viewersname  = $('#viewersname').val();
      $.ajax
        ({
          type: "POST",
          url: "https://meritnotes.com//healper/new_letter_insert.php",
          data: {viewerscomments:viewerscomments,comment_id:comment_id,viewersname:viewersname},
          success: function (data) {
            $('.viewer_comment_result').html(data);
            $('#postcomments')[0].reset();
          }
        });
    });
  });
</script>	    </body>
